***покой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a> (1369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pokojь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>calm, rest, peace</li>
<li>quiet</li>
<li>old name of the letter <b>п</b> in the early Cyrillic alphabet</li>
<li>apartment, room, chamber
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приемный.html>приёмный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijómnyj pokój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">admission department, admission room <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a hospital</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pokojь</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pokojь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойница.html>поко́йница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokójnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойница.html>поко́йницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойница.html>поко́йницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойница.html>поко́йниц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойник.html>поко́йник</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йный</a> (6860)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokójnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поко́йнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поко́йней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> calm, tranquil</li>
<li>late, deceased
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йный</a></b> муж</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">moj <b>pokójnyj</b> muž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my late husband</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokójnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покойный.html>поко́йных</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deceased person</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-покой-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поколебать.html>поколеба́ть</a> (18479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">колеба́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolebátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поколебать.html>поколеба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokolebátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">колеба́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rock, to shake</li>
<li>to shake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:авторитет.html>авторите́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поколебленный.html>поколе́блен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó avtoritét byl pokoléblen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his authority was shaken</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поколебать.html>поколеба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokolebátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поколебаться.html>поколеба́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokolebátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колебаться.html>колеба́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to oscillate, to vibrate, to vacillate, to sway</li>
<li>to fluctuate, to vary</li>
<li>to hesitate, to waver</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поколебать.html>поколеба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokolebátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поколебленный.html>поколе́бленный</a></b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-колебл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-енн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покончить.html>поко́нчить</a> (3645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to finish off, to put an end to something, to do away with something, to be through with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покончить.html>поко́нчить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёты</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо/че́м-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokónčitʹ</b> sčóty (s kém-libo/čém-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break off (with)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покончить.html>поко́нчить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоубийство.html>самоуби́йством</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokónčitʹ</b> žiznʹ samoubíjstvom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to commit suicide</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покончить.html>поко́нчить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>собо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokónčitʹ</b> s sobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to commit suicide</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кон.html>ко́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***покопаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покопаться.html>покопа́ться</a> (16609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копаться.html>копа́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kopátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покопаться.html>покопа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokopátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dig for awhile</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to delve (into) for awhile, to spend some time examining carefully</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покорный.html>поко́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokórnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>submissive <i>(to)</i>, obedient <i>(to)</i>, resigned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покорный.html>поко́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьбе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokórnyj</b> sudʹbé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">resigned to one's fate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ваш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покорный.html>поко́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слуга.html>слуга́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vaš pokórnyj slugá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">your most humble servant; yours truly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слуга.html>слуга́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покорный.html>поко́рный</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slugá pokórnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> it's not for me; I am not having/taking any</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́бить</a> (22191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коробить.html>коро́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koróbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokoróbitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коробить.html>коро́бить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to warp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>до́ску</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́било</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырость.html>сы́рости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dósku <b>pokoróbilo</b> ot sýrosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the board <b>was warped</b> from the dampness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ruin, to disfigure</li>
<li>to grate, to jar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shock, to disgust</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́бленный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokoróblennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">покоро́бленность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokoróblennostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokoróbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покоробить.html>покоро́бленный</a></b>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покоряться.html>покоря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokorjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покориться.html>покори́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to submit (to), to resign oneself to
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1906</b>,  Лидия Дмитриевна Зиновьева-Аннибал (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lydia_Zinovieva-Annibal" class="extiw" title="w:Lydia Zinovieva-Annibal">Lydia Dmitrievna Zinovieva-Annibal</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%A2%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B4%D1%86%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%8C_%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B8_%D1%83%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B4%D0%B0_(%D0%97%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B0-%D0%90%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B1%D0%B0%D0%BB)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Тридцать три урода (Зиновьева-Аннибал)"><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>Три́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:урод.html>уро́да</a></a></cite>  | <cite>Thirty-three Abominations</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>К</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обманывать.html>обма́нывать</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покориться.html>покорю́сь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:конечно.html>коне́чно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ропот.html>ро́пота</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:покориться.html>покорю́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne ljubljú rabótatʹ. K čemú sebjá obmányvatʹ? No, jésli núžno rabótatʹ, ja <b>pokorjúsʹ</b>, konéčno, bez rópota. Tak že <b>pokorjúsʹ</b> i bóli, i smérti.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't like to work. Why should I deceive myself? But if it's necessary to work, I will <b>submit</b>, of course, without grumbling. Just as I <b>submit</b> to pain, and to death.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покорять.html>покоря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pokorjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко́</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краснеть.html>красне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krasnétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покраснеть.html>покрасне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokrasnétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краснеть.html>красне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to redden, to grow red</li>
<li>to blush, to turn red in the face</li></ol>
